  <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
var regionOrientProv = '';
var regionOrientCity = '';
var regionOrientWeatherCity = '';

//start
function getRegionCookie(N) {
	var c = document.cookie.split("; ");
	for(var i = 0; i < c.length; i ++) {
		var d = c[i].split("=");
		if(d[0] == N){
			return unescape(d[1]);
		}
	}
	return "";
}
//Q is 1 min.
function setRegionCookie(N, V, Q) {
	var L = new Date();
	var z = new Date(L.getTime() + Q * 60000);
	var domain = '.ifeng.com';
	document.cookie = N + "=" + escape(V) + ";path=/;domain=" + domain + ";expires=" + z.toGMTString() + ";"
	//document.cookie = N + "=" + escape(V) + ";path=/;expires=" + z.toGMTString() + ";"
};

//callback function----1440 1day; 43200 30days
function setRegionCookies(locationStr){	

	var regionArray = locationStr.split("[");

	var regionStr = regionArray[0].slice(0,-1);
	var regionTempArray = regionStr.split("_");
	var regionProv = regionTempArray[0];
	var regionCity = regionTempArray[1];

	var regionWeatherCity = regionArray[1].slice(0,-1);

	setRegionCookie('prov', regionProv, 43200);
	setRegionCookie('city', regionCity, 43200);	
	setRegionCookie('weather_city', regionWeatherCity, 43200);		
}


//get the region cookie 
regionOrientProv = getRegionCookie('prov');
regionOrientCity = getRegionCookie('city');
regionOrientWeatherCity = getRegionCookie('weather_city');

//test data：Beijing IP：202.112.32.53    Tianjin IP：60.24.101.22

//If there isn't any region cookie value, get the values and then set them in cookie
if (typeof(regionOrientProv) == 'undefined' || typeof(regionOrientCity) == 'undefined' || typeof(regionOrientWeatherCity) == 'undefined'||
	regionOrientProv == 'undefined' || regionOrientProv == '' || regionOrientCity == '' || regionOrientCity == 'undefined' || 
	 regionOrientWeatherCity == '' || regionOrientWeatherCity == 'undefined'  ) {	
	
		document.write('<scr'+'ipt type="text/javascript" src="http://region.ifeng.com/get?format=js&callback=setRegionCookies"><'+'/script>');
		//loadScript("http://region.ifeng.com/get?format=js&callback=setRegionCookies");	
}


//for fix the wrong cookie value problems(will be deleted later)
if (regionOrientWeatherCity != '' ) {
	if (regionOrientWeatherCity.length == 1) {
		document.write('<scr'+'ipt type="text/javascript" src="http://region.ifeng.com/get?format=js&callback=setRegionCookies"><'+'/script>');
	}

	if (regionOrientWeatherCity.length == 2 && regionOrientWeatherCity != 'sh' && regionOrientWeatherCity != 'bj' 
		&& regionOrientWeatherCity != 'tj' && regionOrientWeatherCity != 'am' && regionOrientWeatherCity != 'cq' && regionOrientWeatherCity != 'xg') {
		document.write('<scr'+'ipt type="text/javascript" src="http://region.ifeng.com/get?format=js&callback=setRegionCookies"><'+'/script>');	
	}	
	
}
</script><!--i_ifeng_index_region_js 2010.12.16 09:38:07-->

if(typeof(AdRotator) == 'undefined') {
	var AdRotator = function(RotatorConfig) {
		function getCookie(N) {
			var c = document.cookie.split("; ");
			for(var i = 0; i < c.length; i ++) {
				var d = c[i].split("=");
				if(d[0] == N) {
					return unescape(d[1]);
				}
			}
			return '';
		}
		
		function setCookie(N, V, Q) {
			var L = new Date();	var z = new Date(L.getTime() + Q * 60000);	var domain = '.ifeng.com';
			document.cookie = N + "=" + escape(V) + ";path=/;domain=" + domain + ";expires=" + z.toGMTString() + ";"
		}
	
		(function() {
			var identifier = RotatorConfig.identifier;
			var maxTimes = RotatorConfig.maxTimes;
			var cookieFlag = 'ifengRotator_'+ RotatorConfig.identifier;
	
			var adContent = '';
			var wrapper = document.getElementById(identifier);
			var elements = wrapper.getElementsByTagName('code');
			var fixtures = wrapper.getElementsByTagName('cite');
			var current = getCookie(cookieFlag);
	
			if(typeof(current) === 'undefined' || current === '') {
				//current = parseInt(Math.random() * 100000) % maxTimes;
				current = Math.floor(Math.random() * maxTimes);

			//取广告代码
			if(typeof(elements[current]) != 'undefined') {
				element = elements[current];
				adContent = element.innerHTML;

			if(adContent == '') {
				if(typeof(fixtures[0]) != 'undefined') {
					element = fixtures[0];
					adContent = element.innerHTML;
				}
			}
			adContent = adContent.replace(/<!\-\-BOF/g, '');
			adContent = adContent.replace(/EOF\-\->/g, '');
			
			document.write(adContent);
		})();

<script language="javascript">
if(typeof(AdRotator) == 'undefined') {
	var AdRotator = function(RotatorConfig) {
		function getCookie(N) {
			var c = document.cookie.split("; ");
			for(var i = 0; i < c.length; i ++) {
				var d = c[i].split("=");
				if(d[0] == N) {
					return unescape(d[1]);
				}
			}
			return '';
		}
		
		function setCookie(N, V, Q) {
			var L = new Date();	var z = new Date(L.getTime() + Q * 60000);	var domain = '.ifeng.com';
			document.cookie = N + "=" + escape(V) + ";path=/;domain=" + domain + ";expires=" + z.toGMTString() + ";"
		}
	
		(function() {
			var identifier = RotatorConfig.identifier;
			var maxTimes = RotatorConfig.maxTimes;
			var cookieFlag = 'ifengRotator_'+ RotatorConfig.identifier;
	
			var adContent = '';
			var wrapper = document.getElementById(identifier);
			var elements = wrapper.getElementsByTagName('code');
			var fixtures = wrapper.getElementsByTagName('cite');
			var current = getCookie(cookieFlag);
	
			if(typeof(current) === 'undefined' || current === '') {
				//current = parseInt(Math.random() * 100000) % maxTimes;
				current = Math.floor(Math.random() * maxTimes);
				
			}

			setCookie(cookieFlag, ((parseInt(current) + 1) % maxTimes), 60);
			
			var element;
			//取广告代码
			if(typeof(elements[current]) != 'undefined') {
				element = elements[current];
				adContent = element.innerHTML;
			}
			
			//如果取不到，取铺底代码
			if(adContent == '') {
				if(typeof(fixtures[0]) != 'undefined') {
					element = fixtures[0];
					adContent = element.innerHTML;
				}
			}
			adContent = adContent.replace(/<!\-\-BOF/g, '');
			adContent = adContent.replace(/EOF\-\->/g, '');
			
			document.write(adContent);
		})();
	}
}
new AdRotator({maxTimes : 1, identifier : 'ArpAdPro_2714'});

  <script type="text/javascript">
var regionBizCity = {
	getScript : function(src,callback) {
		var head=document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0];
		var js=document.createElement("script");
		js.setAttribute("src",src);
		js.onload=js.onreadystatechange=function (){
			if(!this.readyState||this.readyState=="loaded"||this.readyState=="complete"){
				head.removeChild(js);
				if(callback) callback();
			}
		}
		head.appendChild(js);
	},
	getCookie : function(N) {
		var c=document.cookie.split("; ");for(var i=0;i<c.length;i++){var d=c[i].split("=");if(d[0]==N){return unescape(d[1]);}}return "";
	},
	setCookie : function(N, V, Q) {
		var L = new Date();var z = new Date(L.getTime() + Q * 60000);var domain = '.ifeng.com';document.cookie = N + "=" + escape(V) + ";path=/;domain=" + domain + ";expires=" + z.toGMTString() + ";";
	},
	check : function() {
		var prov = regionBizCity.getCookie('prov');
		var city = regionBizCity.getCookie('city');
		if(prov == '' || city == '') {
			regionBizCity.getScript('http://region.ifeng.com/get?format=js&callback=setRegionCookies', function(){regionBizCity.start();});
		} else {
			regionBizCity.start();
		}
	},
	start : function() {
		var prov = regionBizCity.getCookie('prov');
		var city = regionBizCity.getCookie('city');
		var prefixUrl = 'http://news.ifeng.com/ssi-incs/cityteam/';
		//	处理导航
		var flagNavigation = prov == "cn022" || prov == "cn023" || prov == "cn0591" || prov == "cn028" || city == "020" || city == "0574";
		var navigationJs = flagNavigation ? 'index_city_region_nav.js' : '';
		
		//	处理城市版块
		var cityJs = '';
		if(prov == "cn022") {
			cityJs = "index_city_region.js";
		} else if(prov == "cn023") {
			cityJs = "index_city_region_chongqing.js";
		} else if(prov == "cn0591") {
			cityJs = "index_city_region_xiamen.js";
		} else if(prov == "cn028") {
			cityJs = "index_city_region_sichuan.js";
		} else if(city == "020") {
			cityJs = "index_city_region_guangzhou.js";
		} else if(city == "0574") {
			cityJs = "index_city_region_ningbo.js";
		} else {
			cityJs = "";
		}
		if(navigationJs !== '') {
			document.write('<scr' + 'ipt type="text/javascript" src="' + prefixUrl + navigationJs + '"></scri' + 'pt>');
		}
		if(cityJs !== '') {
			document.write('<scr' + 'ipt type="text/javascript" src="' + prefixUrl + cityJs + '"></scri' + 'pt>');
		}
	}
};
regionBizCity.check();
</script>

<script language="javascript">
if(typeof(AdRotator) == 'undefined') {
	var AdRotator = function(RotatorConfig) {
		function getCookie(N) {
			var c = document.cookie.split("; ");
			for(var i = 0; i < c.length; i ++) {
				var d = c[i].split("=");
				if(d[0] == N) {
					return unescape(d[1]);
				}
			}
			return '';
		}
		
		function setCookie(N, V, Q) {
			var L = new Date();	var z = new Date(L.getTime() + Q * 60000);	var domain = '.ifeng.com';
			document.cookie = N + "=" + escape(V) + ";path=/;domain=" + domain + ";expires=" + z.toGMTString() + ";"
		}
	
		(function() {
			var identifier = RotatorConfig.identifier;
			var maxTimes = RotatorConfig.maxTimes;
			var cookieFlag = 'ifengRotator_'+ RotatorConfig.identifier;
	
			var adContent = '';
			var wrapper = document.getElementById(identifier);
			var elements = wrapper.getElementsByTagName('code');
			var fixtures = wrapper.getElementsByTagName('cite');
			var current = getCookie(cookieFlag);
	
			if(typeof(current) === 'undefined' || current === '') {
				//current = parseInt(Math.random() * 100000) % maxTimes;
				current = Math.floor(Math.random() * maxTimes);
				
			}

			setCookie(cookieFlag, ((parseInt(current) + 1) % maxTimes), 60);
			
			var element;
			//取广告代码
			if(typeof(elements[current]) != 'undefined') {
				element = elements[current];
				adContent = element.innerHTML;
			}
			
			//如果取不到，取铺底代码
			if(adContent == '') {
				if(typeof(fixtures[0]) != 'undefined') {
					element = fixtures[0];
					adContent = element.innerHTML;
				}
			}
			adContent = adContent.replace(/<!\-\-BOF/g, '');
			adContent = adContent.replace(/EOF\-\->/g, '');
			
			document.write(adContent);
		})();
	}
}
new AdRotator({maxTimes : 3, identifier : 'ArpAdPro_2952'});
</script>

		})();
	}
}

<script language="javascript">
if(typeof(AdRotator) == 'undefined') {
	var AdRotator = function(RotatorConfig) {
		function getCookie(N) {
			var c = document.cookie.split("; ");
			for(var i = 0; i < c.length; i ++) {
				var d = c[i].split("=");
				if(d[0] == N) {
					return unescape(d[1]);
				}
			}
			return '';
		}
		
		function setCookie(N, V, Q) {
			var L = new Date();	var z = new Date(L.getTime() + Q * 60000);	var domain = '.ifeng.com';
			document.cookie = N + "=" + escape(V) + ";path=/;domain=" + domain + ";expires=" + z.toGMTString() + ";"
		}
	
		(function() {
			var identifier = RotatorConfig.identifier;
			var maxTimes = RotatorConfig.maxTimes;
			var cookieFlag = 'ifengRotator_'+ RotatorConfig.identifier;
	
			var adContent = '';
			var wrapper = document.getElementById(identifier);
			var elements = wrapper.getElementsByTagName('code');
			var fixtures = wrapper.getElementsByTagName('cite');
			var current = getCookie(cookieFlag);
	
			if(typeof(current) === 'undefined' || current === '') {
				//current = parseInt(Math.random() * 100000) % maxTimes;
				current = Math.floor(Math.random() * maxTimes);
				
			}

			setCookie(cookieFlag, ((parseInt(current) + 1) % maxTimes), 60);
			
			var element;
			//取广告代码
			if(typeof(elements[current]) != 'undefined') {
				element = elements[current];
				adContent = element.innerHTML;
			}
			
			//如果取不到，取铺底代码
			if(adContent == '') {
				if(typeof(fixtures[0]) != 'undefined') {
					element = fixtures[0];
					adContent = element.innerHTML;
				}
			}
			adContent = adContent.replace(/<!\-\-BOF/g, '');
			adContent = adContent.replace(/EOF\-\->/g, '');
			
			document.write(adContent);
		})();
	}
}
new AdRotator({maxTimes : 3, identifier : 'ArpAdPro_2957'});
</script>

//背投窗口的别名,一般情况下不需要设置;当同时投放多个背投广告而只能弹出一个窗口时，可以对每个背投窗口设置不同的别名来解决
var backwindow_name = '2901';


var backwindow_oPopWin = null;
var backwindow_oPopUrl = '';
var backwindow_pre = 'backwindow_';

if(backwindow_method == 1) {
	if(backwindow_getResFormat(backwindow_advPage) == 'swf') {
		backwindow_href = backwindow_href.replace(/&/g,'%26');
	}
}else if(backwindow_method == 2) {
	backwindow_href = backwindow_href.replace(/&/g,'%26');
}
var backwindow_domain = "http://img.ifeng.com/tres/html/";
var backwindow_popPage = 'pop_page.html';
var backwindow_pageUrl = backwindow_domain + backwindow_popPage + '?' + backwindow_href + '${}' + backwindow_advPage + '${}' + backwindow_isinteract;

//获取投放id
var	backwindow_getFlightID=function(url) {

		var tmp_start = url.indexOf('FlightID=');
		if(tmp_start>0) {
			var tmp_end = url.indexOf('&',tmp_start);
			if(tmp_end>0) {
				return url.substring(tmp_start + 9 ,tmp_end);
			} else {
				return url.substring(tmp_start + 9);
			}
		} else {
			return '';
		}
	}
//获得二级域名
var backwindow_getSecondDomain=function() {
		var arr_domain=document.domain.split(".");
		return arr_domain[0];
	}
if(backwindow_name == '') {
	backwindow_name =  backwindow_pre + backwindow_getSecondDomain();
}else {
	backwindow_name = backwindow_pre + backwindow_name;
}
backwindow_showPopWin();
function backwindow_showPopWin()
{
	try {
		
		backwindow_oPopWin = window.open(backwindow_pageUrl,backwindow_name,"left=4000"+",top=3000"+",width=10,height=10,scrollbars=no,location=no,status=no" );  
		if(backwindow_oPopWin != null) {	
			focus();
			//拦截监测
			document.write("<img style='width:0px;height:0px' src='"+ backwindow_boss +"'></img>");
		}
	} catch(e) {
		
	}
}
function backwindow_getResFormat(filepath){
 
	 //为了避免转义反斜杠出问题，这里将对其进行转换
	 var re = /(\\+)/g; 
	 var filename=filepath.replace(re,"#");
	 //对路径字符串进行剪切截取
	 var one=filename.split("#");
	 //获取数组中最后一个，即文件名
	 var two=one[one.length-1];
	 //再对文件名进行截取，以取得后缀名
	 var three=two.split(".");
	  //获取截取的最后一个字符串，即为后缀名
	 var last=three[three.length-1];
	 last=last.toLowerCase();
	 return last;
}
